<script type="text/javascript">
require([
        'jquery'
], function ($) {
    // sticky filter on mobile
        $(window).load(function(){
            if ($('.toolbar').length > 0) {
                var init_filter_sticky = function() {
                    try {
                        var $obj = $('#layer-product-list > .toolbar.toolbar-products');
                        if (!$obj.prev('.filter-placeholder').length) {
                            $('<div class="filter-placeholder m-0"></div>').insertBefore($obj);
                        }
                        var sticky_height = 0;
                        if($('.page-header.sticky-header').length > 0){
                            sticky_height = $('.page-header.sticky-header .header-main').outerHeight();
                        }
                        var $ph = $obj.prev('.filter-placeholder'),
                                scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop(),
                                offset = sticky_height;
                        if ($ph.offset().top <= scrollTop + offset) {
                            $ph.css('height', $obj.outerHeight() + parseInt($obj.css('margin-bottom')));
                            $obj.addClass('sticky').css('top', offset);
                        } else {
                            $ph.css('height', '');
                            $obj.removeClass('sticky');
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                    }
                };
                if (window.innerWidth < 992) {
                    window.removeEventListener('scroll', init_filter_sticky);
                    window.addEventListener('scroll', init_filter_sticky, {passive: true});
                    init_filter_sticky();
                }
                $(window).on('resize', function() {
                    if (window.innerWidth < 992) {
                        window.removeEventListener('scroll', init_filter_sticky);
                        window.addEventListener('scroll', init_filter_sticky, {passive: true});
                    }else{
                        window.removeEventListener('scroll', init_filter_sticky);
                        $('#layer-product-list > .toolbar.toolbar-products').removeClass('sticky').css('top', '').prev('.filter-placeholder').css('height', '');
                    }
                });
            }
        });
        // filter popup events
        $(document).on('click', '.sidebar-toggle', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var $html = $('html');
            var $obj = $('.columns .mobile-sidebar');
            if (!$obj.parents().find('.sidebar-overlay').length) {
                $('<div class="sidebar-overlay"></div>').insertBefore($obj);
            }
            if($('#ln_overlay').length) {
                var Isloader = $('#ln_overlay').detach();
                if (!$obj.prev('#ln_overlay').length) {
                    Isloader.insertBefore($obj);
                }
            }
            if ($html.hasClass('sidebar-opened')) {
                $html.removeClass('sidebar-opened');
                $('.sidebar-overlay').removeClass('active');
            } else {
                $html.addClass('sidebar-opened');
                $('.sidebar-overlay').addClass('active');
            }
        });

        $(document.body).on('click', '.sidebar-overlay', function() {
            $('html').removeClass('sidebar-opened');
            $('html').removeClass('filter-sidebar-opened');
            $(this).removeClass('active');
        });

        $(window).on('resize', function() {
            if (window.innerWidth > 991) {
                $('.sidebar-overlay').click();
            }
        });
});
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        require(['jquery','matchMedia'], function ($, mediaCheck) {
            "use strict";
            
            function _getAdapt() {
                var responsive = { 992: 'mobile',},
                    $win = $(window),
                    winWidth = $win.prop('innerWidth'),
                    minWidth = 0;
                for (var adapt in responsive) {
                    if ((minWidth <= winWidth) && (winWidth < adapt)) {
                        return adapt;
                    }
                    minWidth = adapt;
                }
                return false;
            }

            function _getMode() {
                var responsive = { 992: 'mobile',};
                var $win = $(window);
                var winWidth = $win.prop('innerWidth');
                var minWidth = 0;
                var adapt = _getAdapt();
                if (adapt !== false) {
                    return responsive[adapt];
                } else {
                    return 'desktop';
                }
            }

            function _desktop() {
                var ddToggle = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"] > .dropdown-toggle');
                if(ddToggle.length > 0) {
                    ddToggle.remove();
                }
                var ddToggleClose = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > .dropdown-toggle-close');
                if(ddToggleClose.length > 0) {
                    ddToggleClose.remove();
                }

                var seeAllLink = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu > .level0.parent > .groupmenu-drop > .see_all_link');
                if(seeAllLink.length > 0) {
                    seeAllLink.remove();
                }

                var seeAllLink1 = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"] .see_all_link');
                if(seeAllLink1.length > 0) {
                    seeAllLink1.remove();
                }

                var seeAllLink2 = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item .menu-tabs .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.tab-item .see_all_link');
                if(seeAllLink2.length > 0) {
                    seeAllLink2.remove();
                }

                if($('.cdz-menu').hasClass('drilldown')){
                    $('.cdz-menu').removeClass('drilldown');
                    $('.cdz-menu').find('.open').hide();
                    $('.cdz-menu').find('.open').removeClass('open');
                }
            }

            function _mobile() {
                var $toggleClose = $('<span class="dropdown-toggle-close">Back</span>');
                var ddToggleClose = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > .dropdown-toggle-close');
                var ddToggleCloseInsertBefore = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > li');

                if(ddToggleClose.length == 0) {
                    $toggleClose.insertBefore(ddToggleCloseInsertBefore);
                }

                $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"]').each(function (i) {
                    var $toggle = $('<span class="dropdown-toggle" />');
                    var ddToggle = $(this).children('.dropdown-toggle');
                    if(ddToggle.length == 0) {
                        $toggle.insertBefore($(this).children('ul'));
                    }

                    var $menuLink = $(this).children('.groupdrop-title.cat-list-title').attr('data-href');
                    var $menuLinkText = $(this).children('.groupdrop-title.cat-list-title').text();
                    var $seeAllLinkHtml = $('<a class="see_all_link" href="' + $menuLink + '"><strong class="name">See all ' + $menuLinkText + '</strong></a>');
                    if($(this).children('ul').find('.see_all_link').length == 0) {
                        $seeAllLinkHtml.insertBefore($(this).children('ul').children('ul.cat-tree.groupmenu-drop'));
                    }
                });

                $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item .menu-tabs .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.tab-item').each(function (i) {
                    var $menuLink = $(this).children('.cdz-link-wrap').children('.cdz-tab-link').attr('href');
                    var $menuLinkText = $(this).children('.cdz-link-wrap').children('.cdz-tab-link').text();
                    var $seeAllLinkHtml = $('<a class="see_all_link" href="' + $menuLink + '"><strong class="name">See all ' + $menuLinkText + '</strong></a>');
                    if($(this).children('.cdz-tab-pane').children('.groupmenu-drop-content').find('.see_all_link').length == 0) {
                        $seeAllLinkHtml.appendTo($(this).children('.cdz-tab-pane').children('.groupmenu-drop-content'));
                    }
                });

                $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu > .level0.parent').each(function (i) {
                    var $menuLink = $(this).children('.menu-link').attr('href');
                    var $menuLinkText = $(this).children('.menu-link').text();
                    var $seeAllLinkHtml = $('<a class="see_all_link" href="' + $menuLink + '"><strong class="name">See all ' + $menuLinkText + '</strong></a>');
                    if($(this).children('.groupmenu-drop').children('.see_all_link').length == 0) {
                        $seeAllLinkHtml.insertBefore($(this).children('.groupmenu-drop').children('li'));
                    }
                });
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {
                var mode = _getMode();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobile();
                } else {
                    _desktop();
                }
            });

            $(window).on('resize', function() {
                var mode = _getMode();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobile();
                } else {
                    _desktop();
                }
            });

            var ddToggle = '.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"] > .dropdown-toggle';
            $(document).delegate(ddToggle, 'click', function () {
                //$(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').toggleClass('open');
                $(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').addClass('open');
            });

            var ddToggleOpen = '.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div.open[class*="col-sm-"] > .dropdown-toggle';
            $(document).delegate(ddToggleOpen, 'click', function () {
                //$(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').toggleClass('open');
                $(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').removeClass('open');
            });

            var ddToggleClose = '.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > .dropdown-toggle-close';
            $(document).delegate(ddToggleClose, 'click', function () {
                $(this).parent('.groupmenu-drop').hide();
                $('.cdz-menu').removeClass('drilldown');
                $(this).parent('.groupmenu-drop').removeClass('open');
                $(this).parent('.groupmenu-drop').parent('.item.level0.level-top').removeClass('open');
            });

            $(document).delegate('.cdz-menu .item.level-top > .dropdown-toggle', 'click', function () {
                var mode = _getMode();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobile();
                    //$('.cdz-menu').toggleClass('drilldown');
                    $('.cdz-menu').addClass('drilldown');
                }
            });

            /*$(document).delegate('.cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0', 'mouseenter', function () {
                $(this).addClass('item-active');
            });

            $(document).delegate('.cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0', 'mouseleave', function () {
                $(this).removeClass('item-active');
            });*/

            /*$('.cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0').hover(function(e) {
                $(this).addClass('item-active');
            }, function(e) {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    $(this).removeClass('item-active');
                }, 300);
            });*/
        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        require(['jquery','matchMedia'], function ($, mediaCheck) {
            "use strict";
            
            function _getAdapt() {
                var responsive = { 992: 'mobile',},
                    $win = $(window),
                    winWidth = $win.prop('innerWidth'),
                    minWidth = 0;
                for (var adapt in responsive) {
                    if ((minWidth <= winWidth) && (winWidth < adapt)) {
                        return adapt;
                    }
                    minWidth = adapt;
                }
                return false;
            }

            function _getMode() {
                var responsive = { 992: 'mobile',};
                var $win = $(window);
                var winWidth = $win.prop('innerWidth');
                var minWidth = 0;
                var adapt = _getAdapt();
                if (adapt !== false) {
                    return responsive[adapt];
                } else {
                    return 'desktop';
                }
            }

            function _desktop() {
                var ddToggle = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"] > .dropdown-toggle');
                if(ddToggle.length > 0) {
                    ddToggle.remove();
                }
                var ddToggleClose = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > .dropdown-toggle-close');
                if(ddToggleClose.length > 0) {
                    ddToggleClose.remove();
                }

                var seeAllLink = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu > .level0.parent > .groupmenu-drop > .see_all_link');
                if(seeAllLink.length > 0) {
                    seeAllLink.remove();
                }

                var seeAllLink1 = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"] .see_all_link');
                if(seeAllLink1.length > 0) {
                    seeAllLink1.remove();
                }

                var seeAllLink2 = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item .menu-tabs .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.tab-item .see_all_link');
                if(seeAllLink2.length > 0) {
                    seeAllLink2.remove();
                }

                if($('.cdz-menu').hasClass('drilldown')){
                    $('.cdz-menu').removeClass('drilldown');
                    $('.cdz-menu').find('.open').hide();
                    $('.cdz-menu').find('.open').removeClass('open');
                }
            }

            function _mobile() {
                var $toggleClose = $('<span class="dropdown-toggle-close">Back</span>');
                var ddToggleClose = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > .dropdown-toggle-close');
                var ddToggleCloseInsertBefore = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > li');

                if(ddToggleClose.length == 0) {
                    $toggleClose.insertBefore(ddToggleCloseInsertBefore);
                }

                $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"]').each(function (i) {
                    var $toggle = $('<span class="dropdown-toggle" />');
                    var ddToggle = $(this).children('.dropdown-toggle');
                    if(ddToggle.length == 0) {
                        $toggle.insertBefore($(this).children('ul'));
                    }

                    var $menuLink = $(this).children('.groupdrop-title.cat-list-title').attr('data-href');
                    var $menuLinkText = $(this).children('.groupdrop-title.cat-list-title').text();
                    var $seeAllLinkHtml = $('<a class="see_all_link" href="' + $menuLink + '"><strong class="name">See all ' + $menuLinkText + '</strong></a>');
                    if($(this).children('ul').find('.see_all_link').length == 0) {
                        $seeAllLinkHtml.insertBefore($(this).children('ul').children('ul.cat-tree.groupmenu-drop'));
                    }
                });

                $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item .menu-tabs .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.tab-item').each(function (i) {
                    var $menuLink = $(this).children('.cdz-link-wrap').children('.cdz-tab-link').attr('href');
                    var $menuLinkText = $(this).children('.cdz-link-wrap').children('.cdz-tab-link').text();
                    var $seeAllLinkHtml = $('<a class="see_all_link" href="' + $menuLink + '"><strong class="name">See all ' + $menuLinkText + '</strong></a>');
                    if($(this).children('.cdz-tab-pane').children('.groupmenu-drop-content').find('.see_all_link').length == 0) {
                        $seeAllLinkHtml.appendTo($(this).children('.cdz-tab-pane').children('.groupmenu-drop-content'));
                    }
                });

                $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu > .level0.parent').each(function (i) {
                    var $menuLink = $(this).children('.menu-link').attr('href');
                    var $menuLinkText = $(this).children('.menu-link').text();
                    var $seeAllLinkHtml = $('<a class="see_all_link" href="' + $menuLink + '"><strong class="name">See all ' + $menuLinkText + '</strong></a>');
                    if($(this).children('.groupmenu-drop').children('.see_all_link').length == 0) {
                        $seeAllLinkHtml.insertBefore($(this).children('.groupmenu-drop').children('li'));
                    }
                });
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {
                var mode = _getMode();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobile();
                } else {
                    _desktop();
                }
            });

            $(window).on('resize', function() {
                var mode = _getMode();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobile();
                } else {
                    _desktop();
                }
            });

            var ddToggle = '.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div[class*="col-sm-"] > .dropdown-toggle';
            $(document).delegate(ddToggle, 'click', function () {
                //$(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').toggleClass('open');
                $(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').addClass('open');
            });

            var ddToggleOpen = '.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop .item.groupmenu-width-24 .item.col-sm-24 .groupmenu-nondrop > .item.text-content > .groupmenu-drop-content .row > div.open[class*="col-sm-"] > .dropdown-toggle';
            $(document).delegate(ddToggleOpen, 'click', function () {
                //$(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').toggleClass('open');
                $(this).parent('div[class*="col-sm-"]').removeClass('open');
            });

            var ddToggleClose = '.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .nav-sections .nav-sections-items .nav-sections-item-content .navigation .cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0 > .groupmenu-drop > .dropdown-toggle-close';
            $(document).delegate(ddToggleClose, 'click', function () {
                $(this).parent('.groupmenu-drop').hide();
                $('.cdz-menu').removeClass('drilldown');
                $(this).parent('.groupmenu-drop').removeClass('open');
                $(this).parent('.groupmenu-drop').parent('.item.level0.level-top').removeClass('open');
            });

            $(document).delegate('.cdz-menu .item.level-top > .dropdown-toggle', 'click', function () {
                var mode = _getMode();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobile();
                    //$('.cdz-menu').toggleClass('drilldown');
                    $('.cdz-menu').addClass('drilldown');
                }
            });

            /*$(document).delegate('.cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0', 'mouseenter', function () {
                $(this).addClass('item-active');
            });

            $(document).delegate('.cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0', 'mouseleave', function () {
                $(this).removeClass('item-active');
            });*/

            /*$('.cdz-menu > ul.groupmenu .level0').hover(function(e) {
                $(this).addClass('item-active');
            }, function(e) {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    $(this).removeClass('item-active');
                }, 300);
            });*/
        });
    </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
  require([
      'jquery'
  ], function ($) {
      $(document).ready(function(){
          $(".drop-menu > a").off("click").on("click", function(){
              if($(this).parent().children(".nav-sections").hasClass("visible")) {
                  $(this).parent().children(".nav-sections").removeClass("visible");
                  $(this).removeClass("active");
              }
              else {
                  $(this).parent().children(".nav-sections").addClass("visible");
                  $(this).addClass("active");
              }
          });
      });
  });
  </script>

                if ($(this).scrollTop() > $headerHeight) {
                    $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7').addClass('stickyscroll');
                    $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-panel-top').hide();
                    //$('.page-wrapper').attr('style', 'padding-top: '+$paddingTop+'px');​
                    $('.page-wrapper').css({
                        'padding-top' : $paddingTop+'px'
                    });
                    if($('body').hasClass('cms-index-index')) {
                        $('.cms-index-index .page-header .drop-menu .nav-sections').hide();
                    }
                } else {
                    $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7').removeClass('stickyscroll');
                    $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-panel-top').show();
                    $('.page-wrapper').removeAttr('style');
                    if($('body').hasClass('cms-index-index')) {
                        $('.cms-index-index .page-header .drop-menu .nav-sections').show();
                    }
                }
            });*/

            $(document).delegate('.cms-index-index.scroll-up .page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu .drop-menu-link', 'click', function () {
                $('.cms-index-index.scroll-up .page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu > .sections.nav-sections').toggle();
            });

            $(document).delegate('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-3.sidebar .drop-menu > a', 'mouseenter', function () {
                $(this).parent().children(".nav-sections").addClass("visible");
                $(this).parent().children(".nav-sections").removeAttr('style');
                $(this).addClass("active");

                var $this = $(this);
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $this.parent().children(".nav-sections").addClass("visible");
                    $this.parent().children(".nav-sections").removeAttr('style');

                    if(!$this.parent().children(".nav-sections").hasClass('navhover')) {
                        $this.parent().children(".nav-sections").removeClass("visible");
                        $this.parent().children(".nav-sections").removeAttr('style');
                        $this.removeClass("active");
                    }
                }, 500);
            });

            function _getAdaptMoveMinicart() {
                var responsive = { 992: 'mobile',},
                    $win = $(window),
                    winWidth = $win.prop('innerWidth'),
                    minWidth = 0;
                for (var adapt in responsive) {
                    if ((minWidth <= winWidth) && (winWidth < adapt)) {
                        return adapt;
                    }
                    minWidth = adapt;
                }
                return false;
            }

            function _getModeMoveMinicart() {
                var responsive = { 992: 'mobile',};
                var $win = $(window);
                var winWidth = $win.prop('innerWidth');
                var minWidth = 0;
                var adapt = _getAdaptMoveMinicart();
                if (adapt !== false) {
                    return responsive[adapt];
                } else {
                    return 'desktop';
                }
            }

            function _desktopMoveMinicart() {
                var minicart = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-9 .menu_right_block .minicart-wrapper');
                var minicartInsertAfter = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-9 .menu_right_block .menu-custom-block-right');

                if(minicart.length == 0) {
                    var minicartMove = $('.page-header.type7 .header-main > .header.content > .header-right > .minicart-wrapper');
                    minicartMove.insertAfter(minicartInsertAfter);
                }

                if($('.page-wrapper .page-header .header-main .header-row .header-right .header-contact .account_block .porto-sicon-box.default-icon.account_info .porto-sicon-default .porto-just-icon-wrapper .porto-icon').length > 0) {
                    $('.page-wrapper .page-header .header-main .header-row .header-right .header-contact .account_block .porto-sicon-box.default-icon.account_info .porto-sicon-default .porto-just-icon-wrapper .porto-icon .porto-icon-user-2').removeAttr('data-action');
                }
            }

            function _mobileMoveMinicart() {
                var minicart = $('.page-header.type7 .header-main > .header.content > .header-right > .minicart-wrapper');
                var minicartInsertAfter = $('.page-header.type7 .header-main > .header.content > .header-right > .header-contact');

                if(minicart.length == 0) {
                    var minicartMove = $('.page-wrapper .page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap > .container > .row > .col-lg-9 .menu_right_block .minicart-wrapper');
                    minicartMove.insertAfter(minicartInsertAfter);
                }

                if($('.page-wrapper .page-header .header-main .header-row .header-right .header-contact .account_block .porto-sicon-box.default-icon.account_info .porto-sicon-default .porto-just-icon-wrapper .porto-icon').length > 0) {
                    $('.page-wrapper .page-header .header-main .header-row .header-right .header-contact .account_block .porto-sicon-box.default-icon.account_info .porto-sicon-default .porto-just-icon-wrapper .porto-icon .porto-icon-user-2').attr('data-action', 'toggle-nav');
                }
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {
                var mode = _getModeMoveMinicart();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobileMoveMinicart();
                } else {
                    _desktopMoveMinicart();
                }
            });

            $(window).on('resize', function() {
                var mode = _getModeMoveMinicart();
                if (mode == 'mobile') {
                    _mobileMoveMinicart();
                } else {
                    _desktopMoveMinicart();
                }
            });

        require(['jquery'], function ($) {
            const body = document.body;
            const scrollUp = "scroll-up";
            const scrollDown = "scroll-down";
            let lastScroll = 0;

            /*$(document).ready(function () {
                var $paddingTop = $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7').outerHeight();
                $('.page-wrapper').css({
                    'padding-top' : $paddingTop+'px'
                });
            });*/

            window.addEventListener("scroll", () => {
                const currentScroll = window.pageYOffset;

                //var $headerHeight = $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7').outerHeight();
                //var $headerHeight = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .header-main').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap').outerHeight());
                var $headerHeight = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top > div').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-panel-top .container').outerHeight());

                /*var $paddingTop = $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7').outerHeight();
                $('.page-wrapper').css({
                    'padding-top' : $paddingTop+'px'
                });*/

                //console.error(currentScroll + ' = ' + $headerHeight);

                if (currentScroll <= 0 || currentScroll <= $headerHeight) {
                    body.classList.remove(scrollUp);
                    if($('body').hasClass('cms-index-index')) {
                        $('.cms-index-index .page-header .drop-menu .nav-sections').show();
                    }

                    //$('.page-wrapper').removeAttr('style');
                    return;
                }

                if (currentScroll > lastScroll && !body.classList.contains(scrollDown)) {
                    var $headerHeight = $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7').outerHeight();
                    var $paddingTop = $headerHeight; // parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .header-main').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap').outerHeight());
                    //$headerHeight = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-panel-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($paddingTop);
                    //$paddingTop = $headerHeight;
                    var $headerHeight = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-panel-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .header-main').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap').outerHeight());

                    //$('.page-wrapper').removeAttr('style');

                    if ($(this).scrollTop() > $headerHeight) {
                        // down
                        body.classList.remove(scrollUp);
                        body.classList.add(scrollDown);

                        /*$('.page-wrapper').css({
                            'padding-top' : $paddingTop+'px'
                        });*/

                        //$('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').hide();
                        $('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').css({
                            'visibility' : 'hidden',
                            'opacity' : '0'
                        });

                        //$('.page-wrapper').removeAttr('style');

                        /*$('.page-wrapper').css({
                            'padding-top' : $paddingTop+'px'
                        });*/

                        if ($('body').hasClass('cms-index-index')) {
                            $('.cms-index-index .page-header .drop-menu .nav-sections').hide();
                        }
                    }
                } else if (
                    currentScroll < lastScroll &&
                    body.classList.contains(scrollDown)
                ) {

                    const mq = window.matchMedia("(min-width: 992px)");

                    var $headerHeight = $('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7').outerHeight();
                    if (mq.matches) {
                        //var $paddingTop = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .header-main').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap').outerHeight());
                        var $paddingTop = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-panel-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .header-main').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-menu-wrap').outerHeight());
                    } else {
                        var $paddingTop = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .header-main').outerHeight());
                    }
                    //$headerHeight = parseFloat($('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($('.page-wrapper header.page-header.type7 .main-panel-top').outerHeight())+parseFloat($paddingTop);
                    //$paddingTop = $headerHeight;

                    // up
                    body.classList.remove(scrollDown);
                    body.classList.add(scrollUp);

                    /*$('.page-wrapper').removeAttr('style');*/

                    //$('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').show();
                    $('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').css({
                        'visibility' : 'visible',
                        'opacity' : '1'
                    });

                    /*$('.page-wrapper').css({
                        'padding-top' : $paddingTop+'px'
                    });*/

                    if($('body').hasClass('cms-index-index')) {
                        $('.cms-index-index .page-header .drop-menu .nav-sections').hide();
                    }
                }
                lastScroll = currentScroll;
            });

            let promotionHeight = $('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').outerHeight();
            $(document).ready(function () {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    if($('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').length == 0) {
                        $('.page-wrapper').addClass('promo_hide');
                    }
                    promotionHeight = $('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top').outerHeight();
                }, 1000);
            });
            $(document).delegate('.page-wrapper .porto-block-html-top .mfp-close', 'click', function () {
                $('.page-wrapper').addClass('promo_hide');
                $('.page-wrapper').attr('data-promo-height', promotionHeight);
            });
        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        require(['jquery', 'Zenon_Headroom/headroom'], function ($, headroom) {
            var configuration = {
                offset: 254,
                tolerance: {
                    "up": 5,
                    "down": 0
                },
                classes: {
                    initial: 'headroom',
                    pinned: 'headroom--pinned',
                    unpinned: 'headroom--unpinned',
                    shouldUnpin: 'headroom--shouldUnpin headroom--scrollingDown',
                    shouldPin: 'headroom--shouldPin headroom--scrollingUp',
                }
            }

            // Element to intialize Headroom on.
            var element = document.querySelector("header")

            var instance = headroom(configuration, element)

            // Dynamically update options after initializing

                $('.main .products.grid .product-items li.product-item:nth-child(7n)').addClass('nth-child-7n');
                $('.main .products.grid .product-items li.product-item:nth-child(7n+1)').addClass('nth-child-7np1');
                $('.main .products.grid .product-items li.product-item:nth-child(8n)').addClass('nth-child-8n');
                $('.main .products.grid .product-items li.product-item:nth-child(8n+1)').addClass('nth-child-8np1');
            });
        </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
    require([
        'jquery'
    ], function ($) {
      var app = {
          isAppleDevice: function() {
            if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(iPhone|iPod|iPad|Safari)/) != null) {
              return true;
            }
            return false;
          }
      }
    // Timer for LEFT time for Dailydeal product
        var _second = 1000;
        var _minute = _second * 60;
        var _hour = _minute * 60;
        var _day = _hour * 24;
        var timer;

        //Set date as magentodatetime
        var date = new Date('2026-05-09 05:45:41');
        if (app.isAppleDevice()) {
          var mdate = '2026-05-09 05:45:41';
          var dateParts = mdate.substring(0,10).split('-');
          var timePart = mdate.substr(11);
          date = dateParts[1] + '/' + dateParts[2] + '/' + dateParts[0] + ' ' + timePart;
          date = new Date(date);
        }
        var l_date = new Date();
        var offset_date = l_date - date;

        function showRemaining()
        {
            $(".sw-dailydeal-wrapper").each(function(){
                var unique_id = $(this).attr("data-unique-id");
                // get Value of dailydeal product
                var cid='countdown_'+unique_id;
                var daysid='countdown_days_'+unique_id;
                var hoursid='countdown_hours_'+unique_id;
                var minutesid='countdown_minutes_'+unique_id;
                var secondsid='countdown_seconds_'+unique_id;

                var startdateid='fromdate_'+unique_id;
                var id='todate_'+unique_id;

                var enddate = new Date($('#'+id).val());
                var dealstartdate=new Date($('#'+startdateid).val());
                if (app.isAppleDevice() && $('#'+id).val() && $('#'+startdateid).val()) {
                  var ledate = $('#'+id).val();
                  var ledateParts = ledate.substring(0,10).split('-');
                  var letimePart = ledate.substr(11);
                  enddate = ledateParts[1] + '/' + ledateParts[2] + '/' + ledateParts[0] + ' ' + letimePart;
                  enddate = new Date(enddate).getTime();

                  var lsdate = $('#'+startdateid).val();
                  var lsdateParts = lsdate.substring(0,10).split('-');
                  var lstimePart = lsdate.substr(11);
                  dealstartdate = lsdateParts[1] + '/' + lsdateParts[2] + '/' + lsdateParts[0] + ' ' + lstimePart;
                  dealstartdate = new Date(dealstartdate).getTime();
                }
                var currentdate=new Date();

                //Get Difference between Two dates
                var distance = enddate - (currentdate - offset_date);

                $('.sw-dailydeal-wrapper').show();

                if (distance < 0) {
                   // clearInterval(timer);
                    $('#expired_'+unique_id).html("<span style='font-size:25px; color:#000;'>EXPIRED!<span>");

                } else if(dealstartdate > currentdate) {
                   $('.countdowncontainer_'+unique_id).hide();
                   var msg="<span style='font-size:15px; color:#000;'> Coming Soon..<br>Deal Start at:<br>"+$('#'+startdateid).val()+"<span>";
                   $('#expired_'+unique_id).html(msg);
                } else {
                    var days = Math.floor(distance / _day);
                    var hours = Math.floor((distance % _day) / _hour);
                    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % _hour) / _minute);
                    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % _minute) / _second);

                    if(hours < 10)
                        hours = "0" + hours;
                    if(minutes < 10)
                        minutes = "0" + minutes;
                    if(seconds < 10)
                        seconds = "0" + seconds;
                    $('.countdowncontainer_'+unique_id).show();
                    $('#'+daysid).html(days);
                    $('#'+hoursid).html(hours);
                    $('#'+minutesid).html(minutes);
                    $('#'+secondsid).html(seconds);
                }
            });
        }

        // Set Interval
        timer = setInterval(function()
        {
            showRemaining();
        }, 1000);
    });
    </script>
</div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        require(['jquery', 'domReady!'], function ($) {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                var allExpend = setInterval(function () {
                    $('#layered-filter-block .filter-content #narrow-by-list .filter-options-item').each(function (i) {
                        $(this).addClass('allow active');
                        $(this).children('.filter-options-title').attr('aria-selected', true);
                        $(this).children('.filter-options-title').attr('aria-expanded', true);
                        $(this).children('.filter-options-content').attr('aria-hidden', false);
                        $(this).children('.filter-options-content').show();
                    });
                }, 1000);

                $('#layered-filter-block .filter-content #narrow-by-list .filter-options-item .filter-options-title').click(function () {
                    clearInterval(allExpend);
                });
            });
        });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    require(['jquery'], function ($) {
        window.addEventListener("scroll", function() { onScrollDiv() });
        window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() { onScrollDiv() });

        function onScrollDiv() {
            var images = document.querySelectorAll('.porto-lazyload');
            for (var i=0, nb=images.length; i <nb; i++) {
                var img = images[i];
                var rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();
                var isVisible = ((rect.top - window.innerHeight) < 500 && (rect.bottom) > -50 ) ? true : false;

                if (isVisible) {
                    //if (!img.src) {
                        img.src = img.dataset.src;
                    //}
                }
            }
        }
    });
</script></footer>
